## <a name="windows-server-2012-extended-rights"></a><span data-ttu-id="c303c-1871">Derechos extendidos de Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c303c-1871">Windows Server 2012 Extended Rights</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c303c-1872">Esta clase contiene los siguientes derechos extendidos para Windows Server 2012:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c303c-1872">This class contains the following extended rights for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
